[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA segmentation fault [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSEGV[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m crash was detected in the Wireshark BAT [0m[1;39m([0m[39mBetter [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApproach To Mobile Ad-hoc Networking[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m VIS dissector during fuzzing operations. The [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrash occurs when processing a crafted test case with the `handler_bat.vis` fuzzer,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically in the `dissect_bat_vis_v24` function at line [0m[1;36m705[0m[39m of `packet-bat.c`. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer detected a wild address read at memory location [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x202020a0030c28[0m[39m`, indicating an attempt to read from an invalid memory address.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a memory safety vulnerability classified as an **AddressSanitizer: SEGV [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mSegmentation Fault[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** with a [0m[32m"wild-addr-read"[0m[39m scariness classification of [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m. The [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrash is caused by a READ memory access to an invalid address, suggesting a [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpotential use of an uninitialized or corrupted pointer.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Technical Details[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe crash occurs during the execution of the BAT VIS [0m[1;39m([0m[39mVersion [0m[1;36m24[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m dissector with [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe following call stack:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The crash originates in `dissect_bat_vis_v24` function at line [0m[1;36m705[0m[39m of [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-bat.c[0m[39m`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The immediate cause is a call to `__fprintf_chk` which attempts to read from an [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvalid memory address[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The signal is triggered during a `QuickCheckForUnpoisonedRegion` operation [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin the printf_common function, indicating that the formatter is trying to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccess invalid memory when processing format string arguments[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fuzzer Input Pattern**: The crash input contains suspicious format string [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifiers including multiple instances of `%x`, `%n`, and `%s`, which are common [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformat string attack patterns:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Multiple `%x` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhex[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m specifiers[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `%n` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwrite specifier[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `%s` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstring specifier[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Pattern: `IXXXX.%x.%x.%x.%x.%x.%x.%x.%x.%x.%x.%x.%n.%sAA[0m[33m...[0m[39m`[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Invalid Memory Address**: The crash attempts to read from address [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x202020a0030c28[0m[39m`, which appears to be constructed from ASCII space characters [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m0x20[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, suggesting potential corruption or misinterpretation of data as a pointer.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Dissector Configuration**: The fuzzer was configured to test specifically the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`bat.vis` dissector with other protocol dissectors disabled [0m[1;39m([0m[39mip, udp, udplite, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mospf, bgp, dhcp, json, snort[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Call Path**: The dissection path goes through:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `dissect_frame` → `call_dissector_work` → `dissect_bat_vis` → [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_bat_vis_v24` → `__fprintf_chk`[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Investigation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis Summary[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I've identified the root [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause and contributing factors for the SEGV crash in the `dissect_bat_vis_v24` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Format String Vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m687[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m704[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m705[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m687[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35msnprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39md_output_buffer, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39md_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[32m"B.A.T.M.A.N. Vis, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mraw_data %s"[0m[39m, vis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` includes untrusted packet data into [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`d_output_buffer` via the `%s` format specifier[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m705[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` uses `d_output_buffer` as a format [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstring rather than as a string argument[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- When the fuzzer provides packet data containing format specifiers like `%x`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`%n`, `%s`, the `fprintf` function interprets these and attempts to read from the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack, causing access to invalid memory addresses [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `[0m[1;36m0x202020a0030c28[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Contributing Issues[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Missing null termination**: `vis_packeth_raw_data` buffer is filled with raw [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m668[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m671[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m but never null-terminated, making `%s` usage and `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcall [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m704[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m undefined behavior[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Offset calculation bug**: Lines [0m[1;36m663[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m664[0m[39m incorrectly increment offset by [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstead of [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`offset++` with `tvb_get_uint32` followed by `offset += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Wrong tree item offsets**: Lines [0m[1;36m691[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m700[0m[39m use incorrect offset values for [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madding protocol tree items[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Missing offset reset**: Unlike v22 and v23, v24 doesn't reset offset after the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Dead debugging code**: The `d_output_buffer`, `vis_packeth_raw_data`, and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fprintf` appear to be leftover debugging code that serves no purpose in the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol dissector[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Remove Format String Vulnerability[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Remove dead debugging code**[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRemove the following declarations and all related usage:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m647[0m[39m: `char vis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1024[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m648[0m[39m: `char d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1024[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m653[0m[39m: `d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;`[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m687[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35msnprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39md_output_buffer, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39md_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[32m"B.A.T.M.A.N. Vis, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mraw_data %s"[0m[39m, vis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m704[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m705[0m[39m: The entire `if` block with `[0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis eliminates the format string vulnerability entirely.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Remove raw_data reading logic**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRemove or refactor lines [0m[1;36m646[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m663[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m671[0m[39m which read the `vis_packeth_raw_data_size` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand populate the `vis_packeth_raw_data` buffer. Since this data is only used in the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnow-removed debugging code, it serves no purpose.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, if the v24 protocol genuinely includes this field in the packet structure,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwe need to properly skip it:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m663[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m664[0m[39m: Fix to `vis_packeth_raw_data_size = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint32[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;`[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m668[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m671[0m[39m: Replace the loop with `offset += vis_packeth_raw_data_size;` to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mskip the raw data bytes[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Fix offset calculations throughout the function**[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFollowing the v23 pattern, restructure the field reading to use explicit offsets:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Read packet fields with explicit offsets [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlike v23[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msender_ip = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_ipv4[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mset_address_tvb[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&vis_packeth->sender_ip, AT_IPv4, [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Determine actual v24 packet structure[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m If v24 has the same structure as v23, use offsets [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m6[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m If v24 starts at offset [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, need to understand why [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte padding/prefix?[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvis_packeth->version = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m or [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m if that's correct for v24[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvis_packeth->gw_class = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m[1;36m5[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m or [0m[1;36m9[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvis_packeth->tq_max = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m or [0m[1;36m10[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m If v24 has raw_data field, read and skip it properly[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muint32_t raw_data_size = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint32[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m or [0m[1;36m11[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Validate size[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mraw_data_size > remaining_bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return [0m[1;35mtvb_captured_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m or appropriate error handling[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Skip raw_data bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdon't read into buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint header_size = [0m[1;36m11[0m[39m + raw_data_size;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m calculate actual v24 header size[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Fix protocol tree building**[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInside the `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block, reset offset to [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m and use explicit offsets like v23:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    proto_item *ti;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    int tree_offset = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Use separate variable for tree display offsets[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Calculate correct packet size for v24[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    int packet_size = [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m or actual v24 header size[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    ti = [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_protocol_format[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree, proto_bat_vis, tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, packet_size,[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                        [0m[32m"B.A.T.M.A.N. Vis, Src: %s"[0m[39m,[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                        [0m[1;35maddress_with_resolution_to_str[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo->pool,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m&vis_packeth->sender_ip[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    bat_vis_tree = [0m[1;35mproto_item_add_subtree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mti, ett_bat_vis[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* items - use tree_offset starting from [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_ipv4[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_vis_tree, hf_bat_vis_vis_orig, tvb, tree_offset, [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msender_ip[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    tree_offset += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_vis_tree, hf_bat_vis_version, tvb, tree_offset, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mENC_BIG_ENDIAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    tree_offset += [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_vis_tree, hf_bat_vis_gwflags, tvb, tree_offset, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mENC_BIG_ENDIAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    tree_offset += [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_vis_tree, hf_bat_max_tq_v23, tvb, tree_offset, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mENC_BIG_ENDIAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    tree_offset += [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m If displaying raw_data is needed, add proper field:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_vis_tree, hf_bat_vis_raw_data, tvb, tree_offset, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mraw_data_size, ENC_NA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Reset offset for subsequent parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlike v23[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset = header_size;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Use calculated v24 header size[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m: Add offset reset after tree block**[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter the `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m702[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[39m* Calculate offset even when we got no tree *[0m[35m/[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset = VIS_PACKET_V24_SIZE;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Define this constant or calculate dynamically[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis ensures the subsequent VIS entry parsing uses the correct offset.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Approach Is Optimal[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates the vulnerability completely**: Removing the format string [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability at its source is the most secure approach[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Follows established patterns**: The v22 and v23 dissectors provide a proven, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafe implementation pattern that v24 should follow[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Minimal impact**: Since the debugging code isn't used in the protocol tree or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many functional logic, removing it has no functional impact[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Prevents future issues**: Removing dead code prevents similar vulnerabilities [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand reduces maintenance burden[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Maintains compatibility**: The fix doesn't change the dissector's ability to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparse v24 packets correctly [0m[1;39m([0m[39monce offset calculations are fixed[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Protocol tree building**: All protocol fields are still added to the tree [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly, just with proper offset management[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **VIS entry parsing**: The remaining packet data parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m711[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m734[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinues to work as before[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Tap functionality**: The `tap_queue_packet` calls remain unchanged[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Version dispatching**: The `dissect_bat_vis` dispatcher [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m429[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continues [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto route v24 packets to this function[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issues[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **SEGV crash**: Eliminated by removing the `fprintf` with format string [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Invalid memory access**: No longer possible since format specifiers in packet [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata are no longer interpreted[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Offset calculation bugs**: Fixed by using explicit offset arithmetic like v23[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Undefined behavior**: Eliminated by not using `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon-null-terminated buffers[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Loss of debug output**: If the `fprintf` output was needed for debugging, it [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be replaced with proper Wireshark logging APIs [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `ws_debug`, `ws_info`[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand should NEVER use packet data in format strings[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Raw data not displayed**: If v24 packets genuinely have a raw_data field that [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be displayed, add a proper field definition [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`hf_bat_vis_raw_data`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and use [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_bytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or `[0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` instead[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Testing needed**: After fixing, v24 packet parsing should be tested to ensure:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Protocol fields are displayed correctly[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - VIS entries are parsed from the correct offset[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No crashes occur with crafted inputs[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe v22 and v23 dissectors [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m439[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m518[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m560[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m639[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m demonstrate the correct [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No use of `fprintf` or format strings with packet data[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Explicit offset calculations without post-increment operators on `tvb_get_*` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Offset reset after tree building block[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Safe use of Wireshark APIs only[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix brings v24 in line with these proven implementations.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
